NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

(In Liquidation)
In the Matter of Companies Act, 1956
IN THE MATTER OF M/s. ABEX & COMPANY (MADRAS) PRIVATE LIMITED
Notice of Members Voluntary Winding up pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956.
Notice is hereby given to all concerned that the above named company having its registered office at G.B. Regent Place,
151, Habibullah Road, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017, was wound up voluntarily by the members passing special resolution
on 5th January 2010 in the Extraordinary general meeting held on that date and Liquidator has been appointed.

Chennai-600 017,
12th January 2010.

For Abex & Company (Madras) Private Limited,
(In Liquidation)
KOSHI PHILIP,
Liquidator.
